Short title; table of contents

Short title
This Act may be cited as the
Miscellaneous Tariff Bill Reform Act

I
Temporary duty suspensions and reductions
10001.
Reference
Except as otherwise expressly provided, whenever in this title an amendment or repeal is expressed in terms of an amendment to, or repeal of, a chapter, subchapter, note, additional U.S. note, heading, subheading, or other provision, the reference shall be considered to be made to a chapter, subchapter, note, additional U.S. note, heading, subheading, or other provision of the Harmonized Tariff Schedule of the United States.

C
Effective date
14001.
Effective date
(a)
In general
The amendments made by this Act apply to articles entered on or after the 30th day after the date of the enactment of this Act.
(b)
Retroactive application
(1)
In general
Notwithstanding section 514 of the Tariff Act of 1930 (
19 U.S.C. 1514
) or any other provision of law and subject to paragraph (2), any entry of an article classifiable under a heading of subchapter II of chapter 99 of the Harmonized Tariff Schedule of the United States added or amended by this Act芒聙聰
(A)
that was made芒聙聰
(i)
on or after January 1, 2021, and
(ii)
before the effective date described in subsection (a), and
(B)
to which a lower rate of duty would apply if the entry were made on or after such effective date,
shall be liquidated or reliquidated as though such entry occurred on such effective date.
(2)
Requests
A liquidation or reliquidation may be made under paragraph (1) with respect to an entry only if a request therefor is filed with U.S. Customs and Border Protection not later than 180 days after the date of the enactment of this Act that contains sufficient information to enable U.S. Customs and Border Protection芒聙聰
(A)
to locate the entry; or
(B)
to reconstruct the entry if it cannot be located.
(3)
Payment of amounts owed
Any amounts owed by the United States pursuant to the liquidation or reliquidation of an entry of a covered article under subparagraph (A) shall be paid, without interest, not later than 90 days after the date of the liquidation or reliquidation (as the case may be).
(c)
Definitions
In this section, the terms
enter
and
entry
include a withdrawal from warehouse for consumption.
14002.
Additional eligibility requirements
Any goods that are entered, or withdrawn from warehouse for consumption, on or after the effective date described in section 14001(a) and that are either芒聙聰
(1)
not subject to additional duties or other restrictions under section 301 of the Trade Act of 1974 (
19 U.S.C. 2411
), or
(2)
subject to additional duties or other restrictions under section 301 of such Act as of the date of entry or withdrawal from warehouse but which have been excluded from the application of such additional duties or other restrictions based upon the coverage of the individual shipment of such goods by a product exclusion announced by the United States Trade Representative on or before December 31, 2020,
shall be eligible to be entered free of duty or at a reduced rate of duty as provided under any provision of subchapter II of chapter 99 added or amended by this title, unless otherwise specified in the article description of such provision.
